msg:Grand Hyatt Sanya Haitang Bay
Some few keys I‚Äôd like to pinpoint during my stay in this resort. We were staying for 5 nights, from June 1st to 8th. 

CLEANLINESS 
I‚Äôm very surprised with the cleanliness in the room and surrounding areas. Walking through the lobby, garden areas, pool areas and of course the room. You‚Äôll be able to see gardeners, housekeepers, and cleaners doing everything to clean the their areas. This resort is spotless. Five stars for that.

LOCATION 
Location is quite far from downtown but enough to go shopping around 68 market/mall. The hotel is connected to the mall where you can find and dine local restaurants. It is good when you‚Äôre trying to avoid the pricy meal at the resort. (Go local, get cheaper)
And yes, location from the airport is about 35-45 minutes away. No traffic on the way. But try to avoid some local drivers who‚Äôs trying to give you a cheaper price to send you to the hotel. Always check the price on Didi or other app. When using those apps there will be no compromise.

SERVICE
Service. Well, overall it was great! Starting from reception, we were greeted during the arrival with the help of our luggage and stuff and guided us through the lobby. The receptionist attended us during check-in was very attentive and helpful (I didn‚Äôt get a chance to check her name). She was very helpful, and even gave us a tour through the map and sent us to the lift to our room. 

The young man and young lady at the housekeeping dept. was always ready to help us with what we needed in the room and prepared a honeymoon decoration in the room on the first day with complementary champagne and a fruit basket (Downside: some are telling to give them five stars) but I totally understand as it helps them as well.

Restaurant staff are relatively friendly and helpful. Very welcoming when you coming for breakfast and guide us to our seats. BUT, you‚Äôll need to come earlier than 9. Otherwise, you‚Äôll be lining up outside the restaurant waiting for the vacant seat.

AMENITIES 
Amenities are well cleaned and new. Showers and tub are quite new and well maintained. Other things in the resort are basically great.
Swimming at the beach is on your own risk. No lifeguard assigned to watch as it is a public beach. Basically it‚Äôs not allowed to go swimming. Haitang bay resorts are all the same. If you‚Äôre looking for a resort where you can swim, you need to find somewhere else such as Yalong bay or Wuzhizhou Island.

Overall stay was great. 
Just bear in mind, if you‚Äôre looking for a hotel or resort for fun this resort is not for you. But if you‚Äôre looking for a relaxation and calm holiday this resort is for you. 
There are only few entertainment and experience you can have in the resort such as live music during barbecue dinner at the Grand Cafe, dinner in the sky, and show outside the restaurant.

The previous InterContinental separated the suite types into a check-in area, and the Grand Hyatt also has many larger units. You may consider learning from this to improve your stay experience.
Room type: The room is spacious, and the suite living room is large and not cramped. The advantage of the dual-connected house type is that you can move in early as long as one room is cleared out. The disadvantage is that there is no strong magnetic suction to hold the door after the connected door is opened. Combined with the wind in Haitang Bay, there is a risk. It is recommended that families with children use heavy chairs to block the door at all times during their stay. It‚Äôs also fun to watch the restaurant in the sky from the balcony.
Activity facilities: There is a gym on the fifth floor of the hotel (it is quite spacious and has a good view), KTV and video game room. When playing games, remember to ask for a card from the front desk on the fifth floor. There are many activities and the indoor and outdoor planning is relatively balanced. Children spend a lot of time there every day. Children also love watching the performances every night, but the speakers are too loud, which is a bit ear-piercing. There is a newly opened go-kart on the large lawn next to the sky restaurant. The price is very good and the speed is extremely slow, which is suitable for children to play.
Swimming pool: There are three swimming pools, and the two constant-temperature pools are quite large. I especially like the children's swimming pool. I saw someone complaining about the maintenance of the children's swimming pool on the Internet before. I checked the hotel's official children's swimming pool and opened it in mid-February. It is very fun. Before moving in in winter, it is recommended to call directly to ask about the status of the swimming pool and constant temperature. The small drawback is that there are no bath towels by the pool, and you need to go to the changing room across the path, which is a bit troublesome.
Service: I received a phone call from Alex from the hotel before check-in. On the day of check-in, the hotel map, facilities, timetable, etc. were quickly sent to me to ensure that we checked in as soon as possible and arranged the six days properly, including the shuttle bus. Alex can be found at any time to help me call. My child was bitten by a mosquito bite in the last hotel.
